 aap unhen pasand karen yaa naapsand lekin aap janamat sarvehnnon ko nazarandaaj nahin kar sakate

 haal main hue sting apareshan ne janamat surveykshanon kii vaidhata par sawaal khadey kar die hai or yah bhi ki kya netaa unamem her-pher karaate hai
 The India Today Conclave mobilized six such people who are deeply involved in the process of election analysis and public opinion poll
 inamen aam aadmi party (aap) ke netaa yogendra yadav, janamat surveykshanon ke agua ashok lahidi, chunaav vishleshak or bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke sadsy ji

 in logon ne kai gambhir sawaalon par vichaar kiyaaru ham kis tarah chunaav pranali ko zyada paardarshee bana sakate hai? kya sabhi janamat surveykshanon par pratibandh laga dena chahie? pichley kuch varshon main akasar janamat surveykshan galat kyon sabit hue hai?pratibandh ke samarthakaes
 Yi kuraishi“sabhi rajnatik partiyaan 1997 or phir 2004 main hamaare paas janamat surveykshanon par puri tarah se roak lagane kii maang lekar ai thim
 When the Election Commission wrote a letter to him in 2013, everyone except one party had demanded a ban on it
 aisa isliye he kyonki ve yah dekh chuke hai ki janamat surveykshan karne vaale unke paas farji surveykshan karne kaa prastaav lekar aate hai
 i don't know how many of you have seen the recent sting operation
 main to tivi se chipka hua tha
 i have often heard that opinion polls have no major impact
 inkaa bada asar kya ho saktaa he? galat soochna ke aadhaar par kisi ek vyakti kaa bhi kisi ke paksh ko vot dena kaaphi he
 This is a corrupt practice under the Representation of the People Act
 ”ji
 V
 el
 Narasimha Rao “congress, BJP and all major parties are the consumers of the research achieved in this way
 aisi koi badi party nahin he jo surveykshan na karwaati ho
 Nevertheless, they are irritated with public opinion polls being published in the media as it may cause them trouble
 ”yogendra yadav“main samajhataa hum ki hamane sting oparation se paryaapt sikh nahin lee he
 It has confirmed many of our serious apprehensions and taught people like us a lesson that we were wrong
 ham yah maanane main galat the ki janamat surveykshan nishpaksh hote hai, kabhi-kabhi galat ho jaaen, vah alag baat he
 Now i understand that such surveys are manipulated systematically
 main self regulation kii vakaalat karata tha, ab mujhe lagata he ki hamen ek bahari regulator kii jarurat he kyonki yah industry khud apane ko regulate karne main vifal rahi he
 There should be a code of conduct
 janamat surveykshan jaanch ke liye uplabdh hone chahie
 It should also be known who has paid for these surveys
 ”surveykshanon ke paksh meshmitabh dube“main maanata hum ki logon ko soochna kaa adhikaar hona chahie, beshak kuch had tak doshapurn suchanaaen mil sakati hai
 i and many other people of this region have pointed fingers towards many such flaws
 misaal ke taur par, meraa maananaa he ki siesds ke chunaav baad kiye jane vaale surveykshan soochna ke beshkeemtee strot sabit hote hai
 The problem is that all these errors can lead to a misleading picture from opinion polls conducted before the election
 ”ashok lahidi“mujhe lagata he ki kisi cheez ke bare main duusare kii raay jaananaa maanav swabhaav he
 The same is true of public opinion polls: voters want to know what other people think about it
 yah jigyaasa itani sammohak hoti he ki media hameshaa janamat surveykshanon or rajnatik tippanee main dilchaspee dikhaata he
 So it is not a good idea to ban it
 jaisaa yogendra ne kaha he, aap ise sirf dabaa-chhipaakar karenge to isse koi uddeshy puraa nahin hoga
